# Fault Localization: iwlwifi Missing PCI Subdevice Entries

- **Repository**: github.com/sg-evals/linux--11a48a5a (mirror of github.com/sg-evals)/linux--11a48a5a (mirror of torvalds/linux)
- **Kernel Version**: 5.6-rc2
- **Difficulty**: expert
- **Category**: fault_localization
- **Subsystem**: Drivers
- **Component**: network-wireless (Intel iwlwifi)

## Bug Report

**Bug ID**: 206661
**Summary**: iwlwifi:9260: missing PCI subdevice entries for 0x2526 (0x04010, 0x4018 and 0x401C)
**Regression**: Yes

I am using Kernel 5.6 RC2 and I am seeing issues where firmware is not being loaded for my Intel Corporation Wireless-AC 9260 card. Attached is the boot logging.

If I can do anything to debug, let me know.

## Task

You are a fault localization agent. Given the bug report above, your task is to identify the **exact source file(s)** and **function(s)/data structure(s)** in the Linux kernel source tree (at `/workspace`) that need to be modified to fix this bug.

You must:
1. Analyze the bug report to understand the symptoms and context
2. Search the kernel source code to identify the relevant subsystem and files
3. Narrow down to the specific file(s) and function(s)/data structure(s) that contain the bug or need modification
4. Write your findings to `/workspace/fault_localization_result.json` in the following format:

```json
{
  "buggy_files": ["path/to/file.c"],
  "buggy_functions": ["function_or_struct_name"],
  "confidence": 0.8,
  "reasoning": "Brief explanation of why these locations are the fault"
}
```

**Important**: Paths should be relative to the kernel source root (e.g., `kernel/sched/core.c`, not `/workspace/kernel/sched/core.c`).

## Success Criteria

- [ ] Correctly identify the buggy file(s)
- [ ] Correctly identify the buggy function(s) or data structure(s)
- [ ] Write results to `/workspace/fault_localization_result.json`
- [ ] Provide reasoning for the localization

- Run `bash /tests/test.sh` to verify your findings

83-assistanttext-
Perfect! I have successfully completed the fault localization analysis. Here's a summary of my findings:

## Fault Localization Summary

**Bug**: Intel iwlwifi driver missing PCI subdevice entries for Wireless-AC 9260 (device 0x2526)

**Location**:
- **File**: `drivers/net/wireless/intel/iwlwifi/pcie/drv.c`
- **Data Structure**: `iwl_dev_info_table` (lines 978-997)

**Root Cause**: 
The kernel driver's device information table is missing three specific PCI subdevice entries (0x0401, 0x4018, and 0x401C) for the Intel Wireless-AC 9260 card. These subdevice IDs identify specific hardware variants that should be mapped to the `iwl9260_2ac_160_cfg` configuration.

**Why This Breaks**:
During boot, the iwlwifi driver uses the `iwl_dev_info_table` to match incoming PCI devices with their appropriate configurations. If a 9260 device has one of these missing subdevice IDs, the driver cannot find a matching entry in the table, preventing proper device initialization and firmware loading.

**Evidence**:
- Current entries for 9260 (0x0010, 0x0014, 0x0018, 0x001C, 0x6010, 0x6014, 0x8010, 0x8014, 0xA014, 0xE010, 0xE014) all use `iwl9260_2ac_160_cfg`
- The missing entries follow the same pattern and should use the same configuration
- Similar entries exist for 9560 device (0x4030) showing the 0x40xx prefix variants are supported elsewhere

The result has been written to `/workspace/fault_localization_result.json` with a confidence of 0.95.

{
  "buggy_files": ["drivers/net/wireless/intel/iwlwifi/pcie/drv.c"],
  "buggy_functions": ["iwl_dev_info_table"],
  "confidence": 0.95,
  "reasoning": "The Intel iwlwifi driver is missing PCI subdevice entries for the Wireless-AC 9260 card (device ID 0x2526). The bug is located in the iwl_dev_info_table array in drivers/net/wireless/intel/iwlwifi/pcie/drv.c. Specifically, the table is missing entries for subdevice IDs 0x0401, 0x4018, and 0x401C that should be mapped to the iwl9260_2ac_160_cfg configuration. These entries follow the same pattern as existing entries for other subdevice IDs (0x0010, 0x0014, 0x0018, 0x001C, 0x6010, 0x6014, 0x8010, 0x8014, 0xA014, 0xE010, 0xE014) which are also configured with iwl9260_2ac_160_cfg. Without these entries, the firmware loader cannot properly identify and initialize the device when the system boots, causing the firmware loading failure reported by the user."
}
